\doxysection{C\+:/\+Users/ivicente/\+Desktop/\+BRANCH\+\_\+\+ACC\+\_\+\+WIFI/src/\+SCE/calib/calib\+\_\+command.h File Reference}
\hypertarget{calib_2calib__command_8h}{}\label{calib_2calib__command_8h}\index{C:/Users/ivicente/Desktop/BRANCH\_ACC\_WIFI/src/SCE/calib/calib\_command.h@{C:/Users/ivicente/Desktop/BRANCH\_ACC\_WIFI/src/SCE/calib/calib\_command.h}}


Microchip Crypto Auth device command object -\/ this is a command builder only, it does not send the command. The result of a command method is a fully formed packet, ready to send to the ATCAIFace object to dispatch.  


{\ttfamily \#include $<$stddef.\+h$>$}\newline

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Microchip Crypto Auth device command object -\/ this is a command builder only, it does not send the command. The result of a command method is a fully formed packet, ready to send to the ATCAIFace object to dispatch. 

This command object supports the ATSHA and ATECC device family. The command list is a superset of all device commands for this family. The command object differentiates the packet contents based on specific device type within the family.

\begin{DoxyCopyright}{Copyright}
(c) 2015-\/2020 Microchip Technology Inc. and its subsidiaries. 
\end{DoxyCopyright}

HMAC mode bit 5\+: Include the first 64 OTP bits (OTP\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} through OTP\mbox{[}7\mbox{]}) in the message.; otherwise, the corresponding message bits are set to zero. If Mode\mbox{[}4\mbox{]} is set, the value of this mode bit is ignored. Not applicable for ATECC508A.

HMAC mode bit 4\+: Include the first 88 OTP bits (OTP\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} through OTP\mbox{[}10\mbox{]}) in the message.; otherwise, the corresponding message bits are set to zero. Not applicable for ATECC508A.
